Could any candidate's terms combine to approximate `exp(-|x|)` exactly (not approximately)? For mathematical equivalence, we need exact equality for all x.

No standard combination of polynomials, logs, sins, cos, or `exp(cx)` can equal `exp(-|x|)` for all x. The function `exp(-|x|)` is not analytic at x=0, so it cannot be represented by any finite combination of analytic functions.
